verification across three main components:\\n\\n## 1. Plugin Manifest Signing (Calculation)\\n\\nThe **Signature** type in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go` implements the **SignatureCalculator** interface and is responsible for calculating the signature state of a plugin during the Bootstrap stage. The **Calculate()** method:\\n\\n- Reads the MANIFEST.txt file from the plugin's filesystem via **ReadPluginManifestFromFS()**\\n- Detects unsigned plugins (when MANIFEST.txt is missing) and returns **SignatureStatusUnsigned**\\n- Calls **readPluginManifest()** to parse the PGP-signed manifest JSON\\n- Validates manifest fields via **validateManifest()** (plugin, version, keyId, time, files, signedByOrg, signedByOrgName, signatureType for v2)\\n- Verifies the PGP signature using **Verify()**, which:\\n  - Retrieves the public key from **KeyRetriever** using the keyId from the manifest\\n  - Uses **openpgp.CheckDetachedSignature()** to verify the signature\\n- Validates v2 manifest format and root URLs matching\\n- Verifies SHA256 hashes of all files listed in the manifest via **verifyHash()**\\n- Detects modified signatures (when file hashes don't match)\\n- Returns **Signature** with status (**Valid**, **Invalid**, **Modified**, or **Unsigned**)\\n\\n## 2. Signature Validation on Load (Enforcement)\\n\\nThe **Validation** type in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go` implements the **Validator** interface and performs signature validation during the Validation stage. The **ValidateSignature()** method:\\n\\n- Returns early if signature is already valid\\n- Inherits signatures from parent plugins for nested child plugins\\n- Allows core plugins without validation\\n- Routes unsigned plugins to the **authorizer** (UnsignedPluginAuthorizer) via **CanLoadPlugin()**\\n- Blocks invalid and modified signatures\\n- Permits unsigned plugins only if authorized (returns nil) or blocks them (returns plugins.Error)\\n\\n## 3. Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement\\n\\nThe **UnsignedPluginAuthorizer** in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go` implements the **PluginLoaderAuthorizer** interface. The **CanLoadPlugin()** method:\\n\\n- Returns true for non-unsigned plugins\\n- Returns true for all plugins in development mode (DevMode)\\n- Returns true if the plugin ID is in the **PluginsAllowUnsigned** list (from config key \\\"allow_loading_unsigned_plugins\\\")\\n- Returns false for unsigned plugins not in the allowlist\\n\\nThe allowlist is populated from configuration in `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go` via **readPluginSettings()**, which reads the comma-separated \\\"allow_loading_unsigned_plugins\\\" key from the [plugins] section.\\n\\n## Key Retrieval System\\n\\nTwo implementations handle public key retrieval:\\n\\n- **Static Keys** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Contains the hardcoded Grafana public key (ID: 7e4d0c6a708866e7)\\n- **Dynamic Keys** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Retrieves keys from grafana.com API (/plugins/ci/keys) with 10-day cache, falls back to static keys if disabled\\n- **Key Retriever Service** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go`): Wrapper that selects between dynamic and static based on configuration\\n\\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline\\n\\nThe signature verification is integrated into the plugin loader pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Discovery Stage**: Finds plugins on disk\\n2. **Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/`):\\n   - **DefaultConstructor.Construct()** calls **signatureCalculator.Calculate()** to compute signature state\\n   - Signature state is attached to the plugin object\\n3. **Validation Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/`):\\n   - Plugin Manifest Signing (Calculation)\\n\\nThe **Signature** type in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go` implements the **SignatureCalculator** interface and is responsible for calculating the signature state of a plugin during the Bootstrap stage. The **Calculate()** method:\\n\\n- Reads the MANIFEST.txt file from the plugin's filesystem via **ReadPluginManifestFromFS()**\\n- Detects unsigned plugins (when MANIFEST.txt is missing) and returns **SignatureStatusUnsigned**\\n- Calls **readPluginManifest()** to parse the PGP-signed manifest JSON\\n- Validates manifest fields via **validateManifest()** (plugin, version, keyId, time, files, signedByOrg, signedByOrgName, signatureType for v2)\\n- Verifies the PGP signature using **Verify()**, which:\\n  - Retrieves the public key from **KeyRetriever** using the keyId from the manifest\\n  - Uses **openpgp.CheckDetachedSignature()** to verify the signature\\n- Validates v2 manifest format and root URLs matching\\n- Verifies SHA256 hashes of all files listed in the manifest via **verifyHash()**\\n- Detects modified signatures (when file hashes don't match)\\n- Returns **Signature** with status (**Valid**, **Invalid**, **Modified**, or **Unsigned**)\\n\\n## 2. Signature Validation on Load (Enforcement)\\n\\nThe **Validation** type in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go` implements the **Validator** interface and performs signature validation during the Validation stage. The **ValidateSignature()** method:\\n\\n- Returns early if signature is already valid\\n- Inherits signatures from parent plugins for nested child plugins\\n- Allows core plugins without validation\\n- Routes unsigned plugins to the **authorizer** (UnsignedPluginAuthorizer) via **CanLoadPlugin()**\\n- Blocks invalid and modified signatures\\n- Permits unsigned plugins only if authorized (returns nil) or blocks them (returns plugins.Error)\\n\\n## 3. Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement\\n\\nThe **UnsignedPluginAuthorizer** in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go` implements the **PluginLoaderAuthorizer** interface. The **CanLoadPlugin()** method:\\n\\n- Returns true for non-unsigned plugins\\n- Returns true for all plugins in development mode (DevMode)\\n- Returns true if the plugin ID is in the **PluginsAllowUnsigned** list (from config key \\\"allow_loading_unsigned_plugins\\\")\\n- Returns false for unsigned plugins not in the allowlist\\n\\nThe allowlist is populated from configuration in `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go` via **readPluginSettings()**, which reads the comma-separated \\\"allow_loading_unsigned_plugins\\\" key from the [plugins] section.\\n\\n## Key Retrieval System\\n\\nTwo implementations handle public key retrieval:\\n\\n- **Static Keys** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Contains the hardcoded Grafana public key (ID: 7e4d0c6a708866e7)\\n- **Dynamic Keys** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Retrieves keys from grafana.com API (/plugins/ci/keys) with 10-day cache, falls back to static keys if disabled\\n- **Key Retriever Service** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go`): Wrapper that selects between dynamic and static based on configuration\\n\\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline\\n\\nThe signature verification is integrated into the plugin loader pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Discovery Stage**: Finds plugins on disk\\n2. **Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/`):\\n   - **DefaultConstructor.Construct()** calls **signatureCalculator.Calculate()** to compute signature state\\n   - Signature state is attached to the plugin object\\n3. **Validation Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/`):\\n   - **PluginSignatureValidator.Validate()** (steps.go) calls **signatureValidator.ValidateSignature()**\\n   - Ensures compliance with signature policies\\n   - Integration layer in `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go` handles error tracking\\n4. **Initialization Stage**: Proceeds only if validation passes\\n\\nThe entire pipeline is orchestrated in `pkg/plugins/manager/loader/loader.go` which chains these stages together, ensuring plugins with invalid or unauthorized unsigned signatures cannot be loaded.\\n\"\n    61→}\n    62→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
